**LogicalStatePayload / LogicalStateRoot.** `LogicalStatePayload` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,bootstrap_phase:Genesis|CheckpointInstalled|Operational|RecoveryReconciling,applied_logical_command_seq,applied_commit_seq,global_transaction_marker_head:StrongMarkerRef?,branch_head_map_root(entries carry StrongMarkerRef),branch_manifest_root,branch_key_epoch_registry_root,key_envelope/grant_registry_root,branch_merge_ledger_root,graph_partition_state_roots,catalog_root,schema_roots,id_allocator_root,identity_continuity_record_ref,constraint_state_roots,resource_ledger_root,privacy_ledger_root,privacy_continuity_record_ref,dp_request_index_root,txn_outcome_index_root,recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryCheckpoint>?,retained_stream_floor,retention_map_root:StrongRef<RetentionMap>,derived_generation_registry_root:StrongRef<DerivedGenerationRegistry>,delivery_lease_registry_root,replay_registry_root,logical_hlc_state,topology_epoch,policy_epoch,revocation_index,replicated_key_wrap/signing/capability-verifier roots,audit_ticket_index_root,audit_root,audit_continuity_record_ref,transparency_root,backup_registry_root,gc_decision_root,remote_retention_authority_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionObligationRoot>,remote_retention_consumer_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionConsumerRoot>,remote_configuration_trust_root:StrongRef<RemoteConfigurationTrustRoot>,sharding_migration_state_ref:StrongRef<ShardingMigrationState>?,config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ConfigPayloadFloor>?}`. `ShardingMigrationState` is `FreezePendingAudit{freeze_ref:StrongRef<ShardingFreezeRecord>}|FrozenVisible{freeze_ref,mirror_applied_ref:AppliedControlRef}|RoleTransitionLocked{begin_ref:StrongRef<BeginRoleTransitionRecord>}|Resolved{terminal_identity}`; no variant names a future command record. Remote roots are empty reserved values before W12 preparation. Fresh bootstrap permits Genesis -> CheckpointInstalled -> Operational; RecoveryReconciling is restore-only and must finish identity/privacy/audit/cursor/prepared reconciliation before Operational. No ordinary work occurs outside Operational. `LogicalStateRoot` is `{payload_ref:StrongRef<LogicalStatePayload>,logical_command_head:StrongCommandRef?}`; fresh genesis alone has no head.

`GenerationRootRef` is the posture-closed union `Local{generation_root:StrongRef}` or `Distributed{manifest_ref:StrongRef<DistributedDerivedGenerationManifest>}`. `DerivedGenerationRegistry` maps a full `DerivedIdentity` strong reference to `{generation_root:GenerationRootRef,global_frontier?,answer_contract:AnswerContract,retention_class,status:Building|Active|Retiring}` and never reconstructs a singular graph/head/schema key. `ShardDerivedComponent` binds `{derived_identity_ref,shard_id,topology_epoch,input_global_batch_interval,resulting_global_frontier,partition_and_authority_coverage,answer_contract,component_root:StrongRef}`; `ShardDerivedComponentCertificate` adds `SameGroupCertificateHeader`, availability/retention floors, and quorum signatures. A meta-local `DistributedDerivedGenerationManifest` is `{derived_identity_ref,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,exact_global_frontier,sorted_component_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardDerivedComponentCertificate>],complete_partition_and_authority_commitment,answer_contract,build_policy_epoch}`. Shard build/advance controls root components in `shard_derived_component_registry_root`; a meta activation control changes `Active` only after every required certified component at one topology/frontier exists. Partial, stale-topology, or mixed-frontier generations remain nonqueryable, and reads use the exact fallback path when the active manifest is missing. Checkpoint/configuration floors, remote grants, topology transfer, backup/replay, and GC retain every Building/Active/Retiring generation through its terminal transition.

**Replica-local RootManifest** is a closed role-tagged union with common `{generation,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,replica_id,group_role:Local|Meta|Shard{shard_id},group_id,filesystem_profile_id,filesystem_instance_digest,local_writer_fence_epoch,metadata_tree_bootstraps[Location|Encoding|KeyOpener],object_location_index_root,local_encoding_root,local_key_opener_root,raft_state_root,nonretaining_predecessor_root_digest}` and exactly one matching posture payload: `Local{logical_state_root_oid:StrongRef<LogicalStateRoot>,prepared_payload_root:StrongRef<PreparedPayloadRoot>,local_applied_logical_command_seq,local_visible_logical_command_seq,local_applied_index,local_durable_index,active_audit_visibility_fence_ref:StrongRef<AuditVisibilityFence>?}`; `Meta{global_state_root_oid:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,meta_prepared_payload_root:StrongRef<MetaPreparedPayloadRoot>,global_applied_logical_command_seq,global_visible_logical_command_seq,meta_applied_index,meta_durable_index,active_global_audit_visibility_fence_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAuditVisibilityFence>?}`; or `Shard{shard_state_root_oid:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,shard_prepared_payload_root:StrongRef<ShardPreparedPayloadRoot>,shard_applied_index,shard_durable_index,global_applied_logical_command_seq,audit_visible_global_prefix}`. The role/group/database tuple must byte-match the rooted `RaftHardState`, snapshot, configuration, prepared-root records, audit fence, and canonical state; cross-role/group substitution is invalid. A `MetadataTreeBootstrap` embeds `{tree_kind,tree_generation,tree_key_id,root_oid,cipher_descriptor,ciphertext_id,encoding_descriptor,placement_records,tree_key_opener,closure_digest}`. Each authenticated internal edge carries `{edge_key_or_range,child_oid,child_cipher_descriptor,child_ciphertext_id,child_encoding_descriptor,child_placement_descriptor,wrapped_child_dek_under_tree_key,child_wrap_profile,child_wrap_aad_bytes?,child_wrap_aad_digest,child_wrap_digest}`. If AAD bytes are omitted, they are reconstructed exactly as `canonical("fgdb:metadata-child-wrap:v1",database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,tree_kind,tree_generation,edge_key_or_range,child_oid,child_ciphertext_id,child_encoding_id,child_placement_id,child_wrap_profile,tree_key_id)`; supplied bytes must equal that transcript. Parent ObjectId is absent because it is not known before parent encoding. The digest cross-checks these usable AAD bytes and is never treated as the AAD itself. This is the exact key-opener path for each independently random child DEK; an opened parent/tree key alone is insufficient. Tree-root bootstrap edges are strong, but ordinary location/encoding/placement/key-opener **entries** are `WeakLocator`/`PhysicalRealizationRef` and do not determine liveness. Semantic/prepared marking first decides which identities live, then resolves their containing realization. The predecessor is `WeakDigest`, not a retention edge. The opened location index supports authenticated nonretaining subobject locators `{container_encoding_id,placement_id,offset,length}` for independently hashed markers.

`MetadataTreeBootstrap.closure_digest` commits only the already-built metadata-tree closure. That same generation MUST NOT contain any entry—strong, weak, or physical-locator—for its current `RootManifest`, `RootSlot`, or bootstrap bytes; the slot bootstrap is the current manifest's sole opener. This is a construction rule in the generated DAG checker, not merely a GC classification.

**ConfigurationState and Raft persistence.** `ConfigurationState` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Local|Meta|Shard{shard_id},group_id,configuration_epoch,form:Stable{voters[],storage_members[]}|Joint{old_voters[],new_voters[],old_storage_members[],new_storage_members[]},sorted_member_descriptors[{member_id,replica_namespace,consensus_signing_key_epoch,payload_receipt_key_epoch,roles,failure_domains[]}],raft_quorum_rule,payload_recoverability_predicate,failure_domain_map,gc_ack_policy,predecessor:WeakConfigurationIdentity?,transition_nonce}`; the ObjectId of these bytes is its identity and is not stored inside itself. Stable/joint quorum validation and the one-member specialization are exactly §14.2. Every same-group receipt/certificate carries `configuration_state_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>` plus `payload_predicate_digest`, and its database/security-namespace/incarnation/role/group must match the enclosing log, hard state, snapshot, prepared root, manifest, and command. Another group imports it only through `RemoteConfigurationRef`, whose signed adoption evidence and retention floor are the explicit nonrecursive trust base; identical member lists, epochs, or a bare config OID never authorize cross-group replay.

Every durable posture has the Raft layer; single node is a one-member configuration. `RaftLogSegment` carries `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Local|Meta|Shard{shard_id},group_id,first_index,last_index,entries[]}`, where every entry signature/digest domain repeats that tuple and an entry is `{index,term,entry_type,command,command_digest}` with the closed tagged command union `LocalTxn{StrongRef<CommitCommand>} | LocalControl{StrongRef<ControlCommand>} | MetaTxn{StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand>} | MetaControl{StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>} | ShardPrepare{StrongRef<ShardPrepareCommand>} | ShardDecisionApply{StrongRef<ShardDecisionApplyCommand>} | ShardControl{StrongRef<ShardControlCommand>}`. The database/incarnation/group-role validator rejects every wrong-domain or wrong-role tag; a shard-local maintenance command has no global semantic sequence and cannot mutate meta-owned state. `RaftHardState` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role,group_id,current_term,voted_for?,log_first/log_last,commit_index,applied_index,visible_index,config_state_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,snapshot_ref?}`.

`RaftSnapshot` is a role-tagged union with common `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role,group_id,last_included_index,term,configuration_at_cut_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,retained_suffix_endpoints,prepared_ownership_floor,certificate_ledger_floor,log_prefix_digest,log_to_state_proof_digest,digest}` and exactly one payload: `Local{last_included_logical_command_seq,last_included_commit_seq,logical_state_root_ref:StrongRef<LogicalStateRoot>,config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ConfigPayloadFloor>,recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<RecoveryCheckpoint>,checkpoint_state_vector_digest}`; `Meta{last_included_global_logical_command_seq,last_included_global_commit_seq,global_logical_hlc,global_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,meta_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>,global_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>,global_checkpoint_state_vector_digest}`; or `Shard{shard_id,through_global_logical_command_seq,through_global_commit_seq,topology_epoch,shard_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,shard_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigPayloadFloor>,shard_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardRecoveryCheckpoint>,shard_checkpoint_state_vector_digest}`. These values equal application through the exact cut; `last_included_index <= visible_index`, no active audit fence is crossed, and later commands/certificates/remote obligations remain retained. Every Local/Meta fence begins `AuditFenceHeader {database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Local|Meta,group_id,proposal_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,post_apply_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,origin_local_writer_fence_epoch,blocked_after_order,blocked_after_raft_index}` and then names ticket, candidate root, and resolution. Non-configuration work requires equal configs. A configuration transition binds its old/joint/new phase; current Raft config equals `post_apply_configuration_ref`, old+new floors/quorums retain the proposal basis, and the mirror orders under post-apply config. Shard is uninhabited. Takeover may preserve an origin-E fence under E+1 only through the exact chain; database/incarnation/role/group and both config refs remain exact, with `origin_epoch <= current_epoch`. `RaftStateRoot` repeats the full database/incarnation/role/group domain and owns hard state, logs, configs, matching snapshot, prepared/certificate ledgers, remote obligations, transition locks, and any fence/candidate. Every protocol reply follows durable publication.

`AuthorityLocalCertificateHeader` is the mandatory prefix of every authority-local quorum-signed receipt, certificate, proof, checkpoint/ack/floor, topology/GC/reconfiguration/activation barrier, and certificate-ledger entry: `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,authority_group_role,authority_group_id,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,payload_predicate_digest,signer_epoch}`. Object-specific schemas below abbreviate it as `SameGroupCertificateHeader`; that alias is valid only inside the owning group. An imported export leaf instead begins `ImportedCertificateDomain {database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,authority_group_role,authority_group_id,authority_configuration_evidence_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,payload_predicate_digest,signer_epoch}` and contains no raw `StrongRef<ConfigurationState>` across groups. The generated certificate-domain checker requires the authority-local transcript, imported embedded canonical configuration, `RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence`, and outer `CertifiedRemoteStrongRef` to agree exactly; old-incarnation, old-configuration, wrong-role, or wrong-predicate substitution fails before object-specific validation.

**W12 global/shard formats (reserved now, activated only by the W12 feature epoch).** There is one meta consensus group and one consensus group per data shard. A raw `StrongRef` never crosses those group boundaries: every registration, basis, routing proof, prepare/decision/checkpoint certificate, fragment batch, apply acknowledgement, or topology proof used by another group is carried as `CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<T>` and therefore has the two-sided retention/GC obligation in the reference contract. All groups remain inside the declared trusted database-process boundary; object-scoped `ShardCryptoCx` unwrap permits reduce accidental key exposure but are not a TEE or shard-compromise-isolation claim. Meta alone owns semantic time and global authority.

`RemoteRetentionObligationRoot` is the authority-group authenticated map `grant_id -> Active{grant_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantRecord>,target_ref:StrongRef,consumer_group_id,minimum_floor}|ReleaseApplied{tombstone_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseTombstone>}|AckPublished{tombstone_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseTombstone>,ack_evidence_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRemoteReleaseAckEvidence>,retain_ack_through}`. Neither terminal state has a strong path to the active record/spec/target. `RemoteRetentionConsumerRoot` is the consumer-group authenticated map `grant_id -> Acquired{grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>,local_consumer_set_commitment}|ReleaseRequested{request_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestRecord>}|ReleaseCertified{request_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestRecord>,request_evidence_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRemoteReleaseRequestEvidence>}|Acknowledged{ack_evidence_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRemoteReleaseAckEvidence>,retire_after_floor}`. The consumer's release-state identity is an already published root/record weak identity strictly before the request spec, never the request's future result. `RemoteRetentionControlSpec` is the closed role-valid union `AcquireGrant{spec_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantSpec>}|RegisterConsumerGrant{grant_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>}|RequestConsumerRelease{spec_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestSpec>}|PublishConsumerReleaseEvidence{request_record_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseRequestRecord>,request_evidence_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRemoteReleaseRequestEvidence>}|ApplyAuthorityRelease{spec_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseApplySpec>}|PublishAuthorityReleaseAck{tombstone_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionReleaseTombstone>,ack_evidence_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRemoteReleaseAckEvidence>}|ConsumeReleaseAck{ack_evidence_ref:StrongRef<CertifiedRemoteReleaseAckEvidence>}` and is included in Local/Meta/Shard control registries. Checkpoint/configuration floors classify every authority/consumer entry plus unpublished certificate-ledger evidence. Crash tests cut before and after all six transitions and every quorum-evidence publication.

Trust-chain compaction also has an input/result split. `RemoteConfigurationTrustRoot` is the consumer-local authenticated map `authority_group_id -> CurrentEvidence{evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>,trust_generation,minimum_consumer_floor}|ValidatedAnchor{anchor_ref:StrongRef<ValidatedRemoteConfigurationAnchor>,trust_generation,minimum_consumer_floor}`; it is strongly rooted in every Local/Meta/Shard payload, covered by every checkpoint/vector/configuration floor, and is the sole selector of current imported trust. `AdvanceRemoteConfigurationEvidenceSpec` is the ordinary role-valid CAS `{authority_group_id,expected_trust_generation,expected_selected_evidence_or_anchor,successor_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>,direct_joint_transition_proof,minimum_consumer_floor}`; apply verifies the exact predecessor/anchor, atomically selects `CurrentEvidence(successor,generation+1)`, and is bundled with Meta shard adoption or shard application of a Meta configuration projection whenever those operations change the referenced configuration. `ValidateRemoteConfigurationAnchorSpec` is `{current_configuration_evidence_ref,ordered_predecessor_evidence_refs,expected_consumer_state,expected_trust_root_generation,expected_current_anchor_digest?,validation_policy_oid,transition_chain_digest}`. Apply verifies every transition while predecessors remain rooted, constructs `ValidatedRemoteConfigurationAnchor {authority_group_id,through_configuration_oid,through_epoch,validated_transition_chain_digest,current_configuration_canonical_bytes,current_configuration_bytes_digest,validation_policy_oid,input_spec_digest:WeakDigest,consumer_applied_identity:WeakAuthorityAppliedIdentity}`, and atomically selects its strong anchor at generation+1. `WeakAuthorityAppliedIdentity = Local{command_oid,logical_command_seq}|Meta{command_oid,global_logical_command_seq}|Shard{command_oid,shard_raft_index}` is nonretaining. A later checkpoint successor or ordinary advance replaces the anchor atomically; no trust gap is legal. The anchor points to neither spec nor predecessor chain, so those inputs can retire after command cut. Both specs are explicit Local/Meta/Shard control variants; no result is prebuilt with its future command.

`TopologyState` is the meta-owned routing authority `{topology_epoch,form:Stable|Joint{old_epoch,new_epoch},partition_scheme:SourceRange{partition_function_oid}|HubVertexCut{vertex_owner_function_oid,edge_owner_function_oid,replicated_hub_profile},meta_group_id,meta_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,sorted_shards[{shard_id,group_id,configuration_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,state:Active|Joining|Draining,failure_domains,key_access_profile}],sorted_range_or_hub_assignments,constraint_owner_function_oid,id_allocation_owner_map,copy_basis_global_prefix?,cutover_global_prefix?,predecessor_topology_identity:WeakDigest?,applied_control_ref:AppliedControlRef?}`. Assignments are total and nonoverlapping, identify one canonical data/edge owner plus explicit read-only replicas, and use imported configuration evidence rooted in `RemoteConfigurationTrustRoot`. `Joint` retains both maps/configurations until its typed retirement floor. A meta configuration transition constructs a same-routing successor with the phase-appropriate meta config; shard adoption constructs a successor replacing exactly one imported shard config. A scalar epoch cannot authorize routing, prepare, ID allocation, constraints, or GC.

**Fresh W12 genesis and one-way Local-to-W12 activation.** `ShardedGenesisCertificate` is the first object in the construction order: `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,genesis_nonce,meta_group_id,meta_configuration_canonical_bytes/digest/payload_predicate,sorted_shards[{shard_id,group_id,configuration_canonical_bytes/digest/payload_predicate,failure_domains,key_access_profile}],topology/partition and initial Topology/Policy/Revocation/KeyManifest/Audit canonical body recipes,initial_global_prefix,root_authority_policy/key_epoch,configured_root_authority_signatures}`. It commits no future evidence, payload, topology, projection, checkpoint, or root ObjectId/digest. Construction is certificate -> per-group Genesis configuration evidence -> consumer-local `GenesisMetaProjectionPayload` objects -> Topology/ActiveMetaProjection roots -> checkpoint/floor/state roots. `GenesisMetaProjectionPayload` is a typed consumer-local leaf closure containing those exact five bodies plus the certificate/evidence refs and availability floor; it has no raw remote-group edge. Every Genesis evidence byte-matches the certificate's role/group entry, and every shard initial floor verifies the reconstructed payload/projection before emitting its barrier. A self-selected member signature or bare digest is not a trust anchor.

Existing Local databases activate W12 only through an offline, fenced migration. `ShardingFreezeSpec {expected_operational_state,expected_logical/commit/HLC prefix,proposed topology/configuration,projection-recipe digests,drain inventory,migration_nonce,terminal_audit_gate}` first rejects new work and drains every active transaction; unadmitted work is explicitly cancelled, every receipted/ordered owner is terminal/transferred, and no earlier audit fence is active. Apply creates `ShardingFreezeRecord {applied_control_ref,frozen candidate identity,prefix,branch/schema/policy/revocation/key/audit/continuity heads,terminal txn/outcome/prepared proof,live cursor/lease/capability inventory,projection recipe digests,migration_nonce,state:FreezePendingAudit}`. Because freeze itself is audited, no projection or lock uses its candidate: external audit CAS and the exact mirror must publish it and clear the fence, producing `FrozenVisible`. Durable cursors, leases, outcomes, replay/backup manifests, and verifier keys remain for projection. `ShardingUnfreezeSpec` is legal only from `FrozenVisible` before the transition-begin record; it resolves the migration state, invalidates recipe generation, and requires a new freeze.

`LocalToGlobalProjection` and sorted `LocalToShardProjection` are sequence-neutral, generated mapping recipes from the exact mirrored frozen Local payload/root/checkpoint/floor. Every source field and mandatory inventory class has one disposition `CopiedToMeta|PartitionedToShard{shard_set}|MigratedLegacy{destination_kind}|RejectedWithBlocker{reason}`; activation permits no blocker. They cover graph/version/constraint state, identity/allocator, branches/merge, keys/envelopes/grants, history/cuts/stream floor, derived/replay/backup, cursor/delivery bytes, outcomes/capabilities, DP/resources, audit/transparency/continuities, prepared/certificate inventories, and remote trust/retention. Each binds source weak identity/digests, destination canonical body recipes/inventory commitments, frozen prefix, topology, and checker version—but no future transition certificate/ref, activation payload/root, checkpoint result, or shard barrier identity/digest. Concrete destination objects are constructed only after certification from these recipes.

After projection recipes validate, the final old-Local consensus entry is `BeginRoleTransitionSpec {expected_frozen_visible_root/head/prefix,projection refs/digests,new meta/shard groups and configurations,expected barrier predicates,migration retention floor,rollback_cutoff,terminal_audit_gate=StructurallyInapplicable{ShardingRoleTransitionAuthority}}`. Its apply creates `BeginRoleTransitionRecord`, advances to `(Lf,Cf,Hf)`, and atomically installs the replicated `RaftRoleTransitionLock` in canonical migration state plus every replica's RaftStateRoot. The previously audited freeze event committed this exact migration nonce/topology/config/projection-recipe set. Once Begin commits, no Local quorum can append or unfreeze; this removes the replica-lock race. `RaftRoleTransitionCertificate` consumes that record and is the dual-domain transcript `{database/security namespace/incarnation,migration_nonce,frozen visible root identity,Begin record weak identity plus command/marker/MMR/checkpoint chain digests,Lf,Cf,Hf,projection refs/digests,old Local/new Meta groups/configs/predicates,fresh log origins,sorted shard configs and expected Operational barrier predicates,topology,external continuity heads,remote grants,coverage proof,rollback cutoff,old-Local quorum signatures,new-Meta quorum signatures}`. It names no future barrier: certificate -> shard projection install -> barrier -> Meta activation. `ShardingMigrationRetentionFloor` and two-sided grants retain old closure. Consumers use only `CertifiedRoleTransitionRef {certificate_ref,old_local_configuration_evidence_ref,new_meta_configuration_evidence_ref,dual_transcript_digest,consumer_group_id}`; both authority chains/signature sets must match.

Activation checkpoints use `CheckpointBasis = Genesis|Global{WeakGlobalCommandIdentity}|LocalActivation{transition/projection commitment,frozen Local weak head,Lf,Cf,Hf}`; shard projection checkpoints use the analogous `LocalActivationProjection` basis. Their vectors/floors are schema-complete body recipes with no future command/root OID. The first Meta entry is `ShardingActivationSpec {transition_certificate_ref,local_to_global_projection_ref,sorted shard Operational barriers,topology body,activation checkpoint/vector/floor recipes,migration floor,expected sequence=Lf+1/commit=Cf,terminal_audit_gate=StructurallyInapplicable{ShardingRoleTransitionAuthority}}`. `LocalActivationBridge` is nonretaining. Apply advances HLC once and installs Operational Global state, legacy outcomes, preserved Local-source delivery/replay/backup objects, topology/trust/key/derived state, and `ShardingActivationRecord`; it fabricates no old Global transaction. After durability, rollback and Local takeover are impossible. Later verified cuts release migration bytes only after independent legacy promises. Every Active Local cursor first replays/ACKs any Local lease, then ordered `PostActivationCursorTransition` rotates authority and creates a Global baseline at the projected frontier; only baseline ACK permits Global deltas. No cursor changes role or coalesces across activation silently.

Arbitrary online activation is prohibited. Operators either run this offline freeze/project/barrier/dual-quorum protocol or clone into a newly created sharded identity. Rolling upgrades within W12 begin only after activation and use ordinary Meta/Shard reconfiguration. Crash tests stop after every freeze, drain, projection, transfer, barrier, role-lock, old/new quorum signature, first Meta append/apply/root publication, and release; they prove one-way rollback, old-writer rejection, exact legacy token/cursor/replay lookup, and no mixed-role visibility.

`GlobalStatePayload` is the schema-complete meta state `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,bootstrap_phase:Genesis|CheckpointInstalled|Operational|RecoveryReconciling,applied_global_logical_command_seq,applied_global_commit_seq,global_logical_hlc_state,global_transaction_marker_head:StrongMarkerRef?,branch_head_map_root,branch_manifest_root,branch_key_epoch_registry_root,key_envelope_registry_root,key_grant_registry_root,global_key_envelope_manifest_root:StrongRef<GlobalKeyEnvelopeManifest>,branch_merge_ledger_root,catalog_root,schema_roots,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,id_allocator_root,identity_continuity_record_ref:StrongRef,global_constraint_state_root,global_constraint_reservation_index_root,global_conflict_index_ref:StrongRef<GlobalConflictIndex>,global_attempt_index_root,global_outcome_directory_root,resource_ledger_root,privacy_ledger_root,privacy_continuity_record_ref:StrongRef,dp_request_index_root,policy_root,policy_epoch,revocation_root,revocation_index,replicated_key_wrap_root,signing_key_root,capability_verifier_root,audit_ticket_index_root,audit_root,audit_continuity_record_ref:StrongRef,transparency_root,global_retained_stream_floor,retention_map_root:StrongRef<RetentionMap>,derived_generation_registry_root:StrongRef<DerivedGenerationRegistry>,delivery_lease_registry_root,replay_registry_root,backup_registry_root,gc_decision_root,remote_retention_authority_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionObligationRoot>,remote_retention_consumer_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionConsumerRoot>,remote_configuration_trust_root:StrongRef<RemoteConfigurationTrustRoot>,global_decision_certificate_registry_root,global_delta_batch_index_root,global_delta_frontier,shard_checkpoint_directory_root,shard_apply_ack_directory_root,global_closed_attempt_floor_ref:StrongRef<ClosedAttemptCompactionFloor>?,global_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>?,meta_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>?}`. Fresh bootstrap permits `(Genesis,None,None) -> (CheckpointInstalled,Some,None) -> (Operational,Some,Some)`; the one-time recovery bridge may enter `RecoveryReconciling` only under the exact restore protocol and must finish its ordered reconciliations before `Operational`. No user/global maintenance acknowledgement is legal before `Operational`. `GlobalOutcomeDirectoryValue = LegacyLocal{outcome_ref:StrongRef<TxnOutcomeRecord>,source_local_prefix,capability_domain_commitment}|W12{outcome_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>}` preserves preactivation token outcomes without fabricating global transaction records. `GlobalTxnRecord` is `{predecessor:ConditionalGlobalCommandRef?,command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand>,decision:Committed|Aborted,assigned_global_logical_command_seq,assigned_global_commit_seq?,global_logical_hlc,marker_ref:StrongMarkerRef?,final_effect_digest,resulting_global_state_payload_digest:WeakDigest}`. `GlobalControlRecord` is `{predecessor:ConditionalGlobalCommandRef?|LocalActivationBridge{transition_certificate_ref:StrongRef<RaftRoleTransitionCertificate>,frozen_local_head:WeakCommandIdentity,Lf,Cf,Hf,local_chain/MMR/checkpoint/projection digests},command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>,kind,assigned_global_logical_command_seq,global_logical_hlc,result_refs[StrongRef],resulting_global_state_payload_digest:WeakDigest}`. Only the first activation record may use this nonretaining bridge; its migration floor, not the weak head, temporarily owns old bytes. Fresh Meta genesis has no head, and every later record uses the normal global predecessor. `GlobalStateRoot` is `{payload_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStatePayload>,global_command_head:StrongGlobalCommandRef?}`. Thus every registration, admission/cancel/read close, policy/key/topology/GC/remote-retention transition, directory publication, decision-certificate/global-delta publication, and activation enters one contiguous meta command-record chain.

Shard canonical state is parallel but deliberately nonsemantic: `ShardLogicalStatePayload` is `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,bootstrap_phase:Genesis|CheckpointInstalled|Operational|RecoveryReconciling,shard_id,topology_epoch,partition_state_roots,shard_constraint_state_root,constraint_reservation_index_root,prepared_attempt_root,applied_decision_index_root,terminal_abort_tombstone_root,fragment_delta_batch_index_root,shard_derived_component_registry_root,shard_key_material_registry_root,active_meta_projection_root:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,global_applied_logical_command_seq,global_applied_commit_seq,meta_policy_epoch,meta_revocation_index,meta_key_epoch_commitment,audit_visible_global_prefix,retention_map_root:StrongRef<RetentionMap>,remote_retention_authority_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionObligationRoot>,remote_retention_consumer_root:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionConsumerRoot>,remote_configuration_trust_root:StrongRef<RemoteConfigurationTrustRoot>,shard_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardRecoveryCheckpoint>?,shard_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigPayloadFloor>?}`; it has fresh three-state bootstrap and restore-only reconciliation, and no work before `Operational`. `ActiveMetaProjectionRoot` maps `Topology|Policy|Revocation|KeyManifest|Audit` to exactly one source: `Genesis{certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardedGenesisCertificate>,payload_ref:StrongRef<GenesisMetaProjectionPayload>,projection_digest}|Activation{transition_ref:CertifiedRoleTransitionRef,projection_ref:StrongRef<LocalToShardProjection>,payload_ref:StrongRef<ActivationMetaProjectionPayload>,projection_digest}|Control{source_global_control_identity,source_global_prefix,payload_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef,projection_digest}`. Genesis/activation payloads are typed consumer-local closures constructed after their certificate and contain no raw remote edge; the first later Meta controls replace/advance them. Aggregate scalars byte-match rooted values and are cross-checks only. `ShardConstraintStateRoot` contains aggregate contributions and prepare-keyed reservation refs; prepare installs and decision consumes/releases them. `ShardCommandRecord` is `{predecessor:ConditionalShardCommandRef?,shard_raft_index,command:StrongRef<ShardPrepareCommand|ShardDecisionApplyCommand|ShardControlCommand>,result_refs[StrongRef],resulting_shard_payload_digest:WeakDigest}`; `ShardLogicalStateRoot` is `{payload_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStatePayload>,shard_command_head:StrongShardCommandRef?}`. Shard order cannot move branch heads or semantic time. Generated checkpoint/floor/backup/GC coverage includes every root above.

Key authority is meta-owned but ciphertext/envelope material follows its data shard. `ShardKeyMaterialProjection` binds `{graph,branch,envelope_epoch,write_key_epoch,assigned_partition_ranges,meta_epoch_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<BranchKeyEpochRecord>,local_envelope/wrap/opener roots,availability_floor}`; `ShardKeyMaterialInventoryCertificate` adds `SameGroupCertificateHeader`, topology, exact local inventory/zero-reference commitments, and quorum signatures. `GlobalKeyEnvelopeManifest` is `{topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,branch_epoch_registry_root:StrongRef,sorted_shard_inventory_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardKeyMaterialInventoryCertificate>],complete_shard_and_range_commitment,meta_grant_root:StrongRef}`. W12 fork/grant/rotation bundles are pre-order objects containing the exact sorted shard inventory certificates and required two-sided grants. Meta activates an epoch only after the complete manifest exists; typed shard projection controls install the matching entries before use. `ShardEffectBasis` binds the exact installed projection, not only an epoch scalar. Key destruction, backup, topology retirement, and GC require certified per-shard zero-reference/release acknowledgements over the complete manifest; generic payload refs cannot substitute.

`GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint` is `{basis:Genesis|Global{basis_global_logical_command_seq,basis_global_commit_seq,covered_global_command:WeakGlobalCommandIdentity?,covered_global_marker:StrongMarkerRef?}|LocalActivation{transition_commitment,frozen_local_head:WeakCommandIdentity,Lf,Cf,Hf,local_projection_digest},basis_payload_digest:WeakDigest,basis_projection_digest,global_logical_hlc_state,topology_epoch,global_checkpoint_state_vector_ref,nonretaining_predecessor_checkpoint_digest}`. `ShardRecoveryCheckpoint` is `{shard_id,basis:Genesis|Shard{basis_shard_raft_index,basis_global logical/commit seq,covered_shard_command:WeakShardCommandIdentity?}|LocalActivationProjection{transition_commitment,local_to_shard_projection_digest,Lf,Cf,Hf},topology_epoch,basis_shard_payload_digest,basis_projection_digest,shard_checkpoint_state_vector_ref,nonretaining_predecessor_checkpoint_digest}`. Each vector has one `CopiedStrong|ProjectedSnapshot|ResetByCheckpointInstall|SelfExcluded|InstallProvisionalCut|ApplyActivationProjection` entry per field. The provisional tag is required exactly for operational replacement retention maps; `ApplyActivationProjection` is legal only under the matching activation basis and classifies every destination field from the pre-certified body recipe without a future result OID. Fresh Genesis forbids both. Checkpoint/floor fields use exact literals. Generated coverage and DAG checkers reject any mixed basis, omitted field, future ref, or result recipe mismatch.

Recovery treats every checkpoint as the **post-install** payload. Ordinary Local/Meta basis `(L0,C0)` reconstructs sequence `L0+1`, commit `C0`, deterministic install HLC, literals/resets/provisional cut, verifies the unique retained install input/record, then replays `L0+2..head`; ordinary Shard basis `R0` analogously reconstructs `R0+1`. LocalActivation reconstructs the first Meta activation at `Lf+1/Cf`; LocalActivationProjection reconstructs the first shard projection-install result at its declared shard index and `Lf/Cf`. In each case the transition certificate/projection recipe and retained input/record are the unique witness; recovery never reapplies it. Double apply, missing/duplicate install, mixed basis, scalar/reset/projection mismatch, or pairing with another root fails closed.

`MetaConfigPayloadFloor` is `{basis global logical/commit/meta-Raft positions,current/prospective configs,current checkpoint weak observation,retained log suffix,typed mandatory inventory,active attempt/conflict/reservation/outcome/audit floors,global retained-stream/delta floor,distributed key/derived floors,unpublished/published certificate floors,remote-retention authority/consumer/pending-publication floors,remote-configuration-trust-root generation/floor,shard checkpoint/apply-ack directories,prepared ownership transfers,reconfiguration/GC/activation/restore in-flight floors,retirement acknowledgements}`. `ShardConfigPayloadFloor` is `{shard/basis Raft/global positions/topology,current/prospective configs,current checkpoint weak observation,retained suffix,typed mandatory inventory,prepared/decision/constraint-reservation floor,fragment batch floor,active-meta-projection floor,shard key/derived component floors,remote-retention authority/consumer/pending-publication floors,remote-configuration-trust-root generation/floor,queryable history,certificate ledger,prepared ownership transfers,reconfiguration/GC/activation/restore floors,retirement acknowledgements}`. The exact versioned field table gives one typed row for every payload and protocol root; values byte-match separate canonical roots and include every unpublished handshake artifact. An unclassified field fails G0, and neither floor may retain a predecessor through the installed checkpoint.

`MetaCheckpointCertificate` is a meta-group object that quorum-signs `{global_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>,basis_global_prefix:{logical,commit},install_global_prefix:{logical=basis.logical+1,commit=basis.commit},install_meta_raft_index,checkpoint_install_record_ref:StrongGlobalCommandRef,installed_global_state_root_ref:StrongRef<GlobalStateRoot>,meta_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,meta_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>?,log_to_state_proof_digest,certificate_ledger_floor,signer_epoch,quorum_signatures}`. `ShardHistoryInventory` is `{shard_id,topology_epoch,queryable_global_prefix_interval,partition_version_roots[StrongRef],key_epoch_roots[StrongRef],tombstone_and_hole_roots[StrongRef],retention_lease_roots[StrongRef],inventory_digest}`. `ShardCheckpointCertificate` is a shard-group object that quorum-signs `{shard_id,shard_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,topology_epoch,basis_shard_raft_index,install_shard_raft_index=basis+1,basis_global_prefix,install_global_prefix,checkpoint_install_record_ref:StrongShardCommandRef,queryable_global_prefix_interval,installed_shard_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,shard_recovery_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardRecoveryCheckpoint>,shard_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<ShardConfigPayloadFloor>?,retained_history_inventory_ref:StrongRef<ShardHistoryInventory>,payload_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<PayloadAvailabilityCertificate>,log_to_state_proof_digest,certificate_ledger_floor,signer_epoch,quorum_signatures}`. Genesis certificates require the optional floor `None`; Operational certificates require `Some`. The interval is valid only when the inventory proves every MVCC version/key needed for each included prefix. A database snapshot at `P` requires the meta root at `P` and, for every routed shard, a certified checkpoint whose queryable interval contains `P`; “checkpoint at or beyond P” alone is insufficient.

`MetaRelevanceRangeProof` is `{meta_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,target_shard_id,prior_global_prefix:{logical,commit},resulting_global_prefix:{logical,commit},sorted_command_entries[{global_logical_seq,command_kind,terminal_kind:Control|CommittedTxn|AbortedTxn,assigned_global_commit_seq?,routing_or_scope_commitment,topology_epoch,policy_epoch,revocation_index,key_epoch_commitment,audit_fence_effect}],irrelevance_checker_version,result:Irrelevant,signer_epoch,quorum_signatures}`. Entries are contiguous and exhaustive from `prior.logical+1` through `resulting.logical`; commit sequence increments exactly on `CommittedTxn` and is unchanged on controls/aborts. Only a proof whose entries show no target data, topology, policy, revocation, key, remote-retention, admission/decision, or audit-fence effect may update both shard prefix scalars. Any relevant entry requires its typed apply command.

`MetaCertificateLedger` and `ShardCertificateLedger` are replica-local immutable maps rooted by the role's `RaftStateRoot`. Each entry is `{certificate_kind,certificate_ref:StrongRef,authority_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,subject_identity,base_closure_inventory_digest,first_required_index,release_condition,successor_or_publication_status}`; a successor may strengthen but never shorten its closure or release condition. Meta ledgers retain un-published global decisions and remote-reference availability promises; shard ledgers retain prepare/checkpoint/applied-ack certificates. A certificate may leave the ledger only after its canonical publication/replacement is rooted and every named consumer/configuration/GC floor has acknowledged that transfer. The matching config floor and Raft snapshot carry the ledger floor, so log truncation cannot orphan a certificate between creation and publication.

`PreparedRootEntry` is the closed union `Owned{ownership_id,record_ref:StrongRef<PreparedCommitRecord|MetaPreparedCommandRecord|ShardPreparedPayloadRecord>}|Transferring{old_ownership_id,new_ownership_id,transfer_record_ref:StrongRef<PreparedOwnershipTransferRecord>}|Transferred{new_ownership_id,new_record_ref:StrongRef,transfer_identity:WeakDigest}`. `PreparedPayloadRoot` is the local authenticated object `{database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Local,group_id,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,published_under_fence_epoch,root_generation,entries[stable_command_identity -> PreparedRootEntry],nonretaining_predecessor_digest}`; Meta/Shard use the same header and their attempt/control or `ShardCommandIdentity` key. Keys are unique. Normal successors preserve identity/base/config; reconfiguration atomically changes `Owned(old)` to `Transferring` only after old+new availability exists, then to `Transferred/Owned(new)` after the transition floor and Raft/snapshot acknowledgement. Old ownership releases only after the canonical applied root/certificate ledger or completed transfer owns everything. Abandonment requires fenced proof of non-order. Database/incarnation/role/group always match `RootManifest`/`RaftStateRoot`; entry config either equals current or is covered by an explicit transfer record. Ordinarily `published_under_fence_epoch` equals the manifest. The sole takeover exception preserves the exact epoch-E root OID/entries under E+1 via the takeover proof, then the first ordinary successor reheaders unchanged entries at E+1 before mutation. New records/receipts require E+1; old records remain obligations. Crash tests cover takeover and every transfer phase for Preparing/Receipted/Ordered/committed-unapplied/audit-fenced states.

Replica-local `MetaPreparedCommandRecord` is `{prepared_ownership_id,record_generation,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<MetaPreparedCommandRecord>?,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Meta,group_id,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,payload_predicate_digest,local_writer_fence_epoch,attempt_or_control_identity,base_closure_inventory_digest,current_closure_inventory_digest,strong_local_refs[StrongRef],certified_remote_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],exact_realizations[],command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand|GlobalControlCommand>?,status:Preparing|Receipted|Ordered{raft_index}|Applied{global_logical_command_seq}|Abandoned{fence_and_nonorder_proof}}`; ownership IDs, receipts, and successors bind the full domain/config/predicate header, preserve the base, and strengthen current closure. `MetaPreCommandBaseAvailabilityCertificate` begins `SameGroupCertificateHeader` and carries `{prepared_ownership_id,attempt_or_control_identity,base_closure_inventory_digest,sorted_payload_receipts,covered_object_kinds,exclusion_rule:Exactly{ThisCertificate,FutureMetaCommand}}`. It covers only already-built evidence/base closure and excludes itself/future command; after command construction, every proposer root-publishes the stable-owner successor that adds it.

Replica-local `ShardPreparedPayloadRecord` is `{prepared_ownership_id,record_generation,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<ShardPreparedPayloadRecord>?,database_id,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,group_role:Shard{shard_id},group_id,configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,payload_predicate_digest,local_writer_fence_epoch,shard_command_identity:ShardCommandIdentity,base_closure_inventory_digest,current_closure_inventory_digest,strong_local_refs[StrongRef],certified_remote_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],exact_realizations[],command_ref:StrongRef<ShardPrepareCommand|ShardDecisionApplyCommand|ShardControlCommand>?,status:Preparing|Receipted|Ordered{raft_index}|Applied{shard_raft_index}|Abandoned{fence_and_nonorder_proof}}`. Ownership IDs and receipts bind the entire domain/config/predicate header. `ShardPreCommandBaseAvailabilityCertificate` begins `SameGroupCertificateHeader` and carries `{prepared_ownership_id,shard_command_identity,base_closure_inventory_digest,sorted_payload_receipts,covered_object_kinds,exclusion_rule:Exactly{ThisCertificate,FutureShardCommand}}`. For prepare, generated coverage includes exact basis/fragment/admission closure formerly called `ShardPayloadAvailabilityCertificate`; that name is an alias, not a second certificate. Decision-apply and every payload-bearing shard control use the same exact-configuration D1 barrier. A stable-owner successor adds the completed command before proposal. Replica fence epochs never enter canonical semantic objects.

`AuthorityPermitRef` is the closed durable tag `ReadOnly{permit_ref:StrongRef<ReadPermitRecord>} | ReadWrite{permit_ref:StrongRef<MutationPermitRecord>}`. `GlobalAttemptRegistrationSpec` is sequence-neutral `{global_txn_id,txn_token,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,operation_class:ReadOnly|ReadWrite,requested_snapshot_selector,minimum_acceptable_snapshot,authority_permit_ref:AuthorityPermitRef,non_widenable_authority_ceiling_digest,policy_epoch,revocation_index,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,registration_generation,terminal_audit_gate}`; tag/class mismatch is invalid. It is applied only through `GlobalControlCommand(kind=RegisterAttempt)`. Apply rejects a selected snapshot below `GlobalConflictIndex.safe_snapshot_frontier`, assigns a snapshot no later than the resulting registration prefix, atomically inserts an `Active` conflict-index vertex, and constructs `GlobalAttemptRegistration {command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlCommand>,global_txn_id,txn_token,database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,operation_class,registered_snapshot,registered_at_global_logical_command_seq,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,tenant,principal,authority_ceiling_digest,permit_scope_digest,policy_epoch,revocation_index,registration_generation}` plus the `Registered` global outcome before payload→control-record→root. Every SERIALIZABLE transaction, including read-only work, must complete this order before its first participant read; no late-registration or ambient “safe snapshot” exception exists.

`ShardReadWitnessBasis` is the shard-owned `{registration_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,shard_id,shard_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,topology_epoch,registered_snapshot,registration_global_prefix,active_meta_projection_root_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,policy_epoch,revocation_index,key_epoch_commitment,audit_visible_prefix,read_state_root_ref:StrongRef<ShardLogicalStateRoot>,read_state_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<ShardCheckpointCertificate>,read_index_or_applied_prefix_proof,queryable_history_inventory_ref:StrongRef<ShardHistoryInventory>,exact_read_graph_bindings,read_witness_refs[StrongRef],final_read_summary,result_answer_contract,canonical_result_fragment_digest,read_authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<ReadAuthorizationDecisionRecord>,authority_projection_digest,recompute_verifier_version,basis_digest}`. Before any shard read, the active meta projection must cover at least the registration prefix with exact topology/policy/revocation/key/audit values; the shard rechecks current revocation before exporting. The checkpoint/inventory interval contains the registered snapshot, the ReadIndex/applied-prefix proof binds that root under the exact configuration, and the read authorization decision byte-matches the full projection and disclosure contract. Quorum export/CRSR commits the entire basis. It contains no write coordinate, delta template, resource mutation, or fabricated empty effect. `ReadParticipantRoutingCertificate` is meta-owned `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,sorted_read_basis_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardReadWitnessBasis>],sorted_participants,complete_read_footprint,partition_derivation_proof_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingDerivationProof>,complete_participant_commitment,aggregate_read_state_cut_commitment,aggregate_read_witness_commitment,result_answer_contract,canonical_result_digest}`. The proof reaches a fixed point over every routed read/expansion/constraint-disclosure source, and the certificate owns the remote state/witness/security bases through the read-close/conflict-retention floor.

`GlobalPrepareAdmissionSpec` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,expected_attempt_state:Active,admission_generation,routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>,sorted_participants,sorted_constraint_owners,sorted_basis_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>],meta_constraint_reservation_requests[],global_authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAuthorizationDecisionRecord>,resource_transition_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],global_outcome_preparation_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord>,pending_transaction_audit_ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,transaction_audit_basis_commitment,global_final_effect_digest,expected_branch_heads[WeakMarkerIdentity],expected_branch_key_epochs,expected_topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,expected_policy_epoch,expected_revocation_index,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity,terminal_audit_gate:TerminalAuditGate}`. The final gate audits the admission control transition itself; the transaction has only a pending ticket/basis until certification chooses Commit or Abort. Apply requires ReadWrite, exact fixed-point/evidence equality, no prior admission/terminal, and current authorization/resource/outcome/audit state; it atomically changes attempt/conflict state to `PrepareAdmitted`, creates meta reservations, installs the admitted outcome state with pending ticket, and publishes the unique admission record. Routing, participants, bases, owner requests, ticket/basis, or generation cannot change afterward. Rebase/topology drift requires explicit admitted abort, release acknowledgement, and a new registration generation.

`GlobalAttemptCancelSpec` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,expected_attempt_state:Active,expected_absent_admission_generation,stable_reason,no_effect_proof_ref:StrongRef,authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<AuthorizationDecisionRecord>,resource_release_refs[StrongRef<ResourceLedgerTransition>],terminal_audit_gate:TerminalAuditGate,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity}`. `GlobalControlCommand(kind=CancelActiveAttempt)` is valid only before admission, proves there can be no shard prepare under this registration generation, installs terminal `Aborted`, closes its conflict vertex, and releases only the named no-effect obligations. It is the deterministic recovery path for client death before admission; clock timeout is not a transition.

`GlobalReadCloseSpec` is `{registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,read_routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ReadParticipantRoutingCertificate>,final_read_witness_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],distributed_serialization_certificate_ref:StrongRef<DistributedSerializationCertificate>,canonical_result_digest,result_answer_contract,expected_conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity,terminal_audit_gate}`. `GlobalControlCommand(kind=ReadClose)` requires `operation_class=ReadOnly`, installs the exact `ReadClosed` outcome and retained conflict/witness/security edges before any buffered result is returned, and advances GlobalLogicalCommandSeq/HLC but not GlobalCommitSeq. The general `GlobalControlCommand` is `{command_version,kind,typed_payload_ref:StrongRef<GlobalSequenceNeutralSpec>,expected_global_logical_command_seq,expected_state_conditions[],proposed_physical_hlc,authorization_decision_ref:StrongRef<AuthorizationDecisionRecord>,terminal_audit_gate,meta_pre_command_base_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<MetaPreCommandBaseAvailabilityCertificate>}`. Every payload-bearing kind has exact pre-command closure coverage.

`GlobalDerivedGenerationActivationSpec` is `{derived_identity_ref,manifest_ref:StrongRef<DistributedDerivedGenerationManifest>,expected_registry_generation,expected_prior_active_generation?,expected_topology_ref,exact_global_frontier,answer_contract,old_generation_transition:KeepActiveUntilSwap|RetireAfterFloor,terminal_audit_gate}`; apply verifies a complete one-frontier component set, atomically selects it Active, and moves the old generation to Retiring without a query-visible gap. `GlobalBranchKeyBundleSpec` is the tagged W12 union `Fork|Grant|Rotate`, each carrying the corresponding pre-order branch/key body, `GlobalKeyEnvelopeManifest`, exact sorted `ShardKeyMaterialInventoryCertificate` CRSRs and remote grants, expected topology/prior branch-key registry and head epochs, complete affected-range commitment, activation CAS, and terminal audit gate. Apply changes meta authority only after every shard inventory exists; shard installation remains the typed projection path.

`GlobalSequenceNeutralSpec` is the closed union of exactly: `GlobalAttemptRegistrationSpec`, `GlobalPrepareAdmissionSpec`, `GlobalAttemptCancelSpec`, `GlobalReadCloseSpec`, `GlobalDecisionCertificatePublishSpec`, `GlobalDeltaPublishSpec`, `PublishShardCheckpointCertificateSpec`, `PublishShardAppliedAckSpec`, `GlobalClosedAttemptFloorInstallSpec`, `GlobalCheckpointInstallSpec`, `MetaInitialFloorInstallSpec`, `GlobalHistoryCutActivationSpec`, `RemoteRetentionControlSpec`, `AdvanceRemoteConfigurationEvidenceSpec`, `ValidateRemoteConfigurationAnchorSpec`, `ShardingActivationSpec`, `MetaConfigurationTransitionSpec`, `ShardReconfigurationAuthorizationSpec`, `ShardConfigurationAdoptionSpec`, `GlobalGcAuthorizationSpec`, `GlobalGcCompletionSpec`, `GlobalDerivedGenerationActivationSpec`, `GlobalBranchKeyBundleSpec`, `TopologyCopyBeginSpec`, `TopologyCutoverSpec`, `TopologyRetireOldSpec`, and the exact schema/policy/revocation/ID/resource/privacy/DP/audit/backup/restore/merge lifecycle specs whose authority is Meta. Each tag has one generated spec/result/posture compatibility row; undefined, unregistered, duplicate, or ambient evidence is G0-invalid, and no spec names its future result.

`GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord` is the sequence-neutral W12 terminal compare contract `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,attempt_key:{global_txn_id,registration_generation},txn_token,registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,expected_registered_outcome_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>,admission_generation,terminal_domain:CommitIfCertifiedElseAbort{global_final_effect_digest,allowed_stable_abort_reason_classes},authority/resource/audit_basis_commitment}`. It names neither the future admission spec/outcome nor an applied record. Admission verifies the expected `Registered` predecessor and installs `PrepareAdmitted`; the later global transaction command must present the same record and transition only that exact admission generation to one allowed terminal.

`GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord` is the canonical index value `{database_security_namespace_id,cluster_incarnation,global_txn_id,registration_generation,txn_token,tenant,principal,authority_ceiling_digest,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnOutcomeRecord>?,state:Registered{registration_ref,applied_control_ref}|PrepareAdmitted{admission_spec_ref,admission_generation,pending_audit_ticket_ref:StrongRef<AuditTicket>,audit_basis_commitment,applied_control_ref}|Committed{marker_ref,final_effect_digest,global_txn_command_ref,applied global logical/commit seq}|Aborted{reason_class,applied_abort_ref}|ReadClosed{read_close_spec_ref,applied_control_ref,canonical_result_digest},audit_state:PendingTicket|Terminal{outcome},minimum_lookup_retention_floor}`. Its predecessor is the immediately prior lifecycle record; no state names its future Global record. `PrepareAdmitted` must be Pending, and only a terminal transition replaces it with the exact matching terminal audit outcome. `GlobalAttemptIndex` maps `(global_txn_id,registration_generation)` to Active/PrepareAdmitted/Terminal and `GlobalTxnOutcomeIndex` maps the scoped token to the same latest outcome. Both transition atomically with `GlobalConflictIndex`; matching terminal retries are no-ops, conflicts fail, and capability-safe status resolves this record rather than a local-only outcome.

`GlobalCheckpointInstallSpec` is `{basis_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,basis_global_logical_command_seq,basis_global_commit_seq,basis_payload_digest:WeakDigest,basis_projection_digest,checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>,checkpoint_state_vector_digest,paired_meta_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>?,retention_cut_body_ref:StrongRef<RetentionCutBody>?,reset_field_tags[],terminal_audit_gate}`. Genesis alone uses no cut body and produces `CheckpointInstalled`; an operational replacement requires the body and paired floor, atomically installs the matching provisional cut, and preserves `Operational`. `ShardOperationalBootstrapBarrier` is a certified leaf with `SameGroupCertificateHeader` plus `{shard_id,topology_epoch,operational_shard_state_root_identity,checkpoint_certificate_identity,installed_global_prefix,history_interval,remote_trust_root_digest,signature}`. `MetaInitialFloorInstallSpec` is `{checkpoint_installed_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>,checkpoint_state_vector_digest,initial_meta_config_payload_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>,initial_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,sorted_active_shard_barrier_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardOperationalBootstrapBarrier>],expected_global_logical_command_seq,terminal_audit_gate}` and is the sole fresh `CheckpointInstalled -> Operational` transition. The barrier set equals every and only `Active` topology entry, all at one global prefix; `Joining` shards are unroutable. `GlobalHistoryCutActivationSpec` is `{provisional_cut_ref:StrongRef<ProvisionalRetentionCutSet>,checkpoint_install_record_ref:StrongGlobalCommandRef,expected_retention_map_basis:WeakStateIdentity,verified_contiguous_suffix_start,terminal_audit_gate}` and only strengthens that exact provisional set to `ActivatedRetentionCutSet`.

Meta-owned directories change only through typed CAS controls. `PublishShardCheckpointCertificateSpec` is `{checkpoint_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardCheckpointCertificate>,expected_topology_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,expected_shard_configuration_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,expected_prior_directory_value:WeakDigest?,required_remote_grant_ref:StrongRef<RemoteRetentionGrantEvidence>,terminal_audit_gate}`; apply byte-matches shard/config/topology/prefix/history interval and installs the exact CRSR. `PublishShardAppliedAckSpec` similarly binds `{ack_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardAppliedAck>,prepare_key,decision_record_identity,decision_publish_record_identity,expected_topology/configuration,expected_prior_directory_value,required_remote_grant_ref,terminal_audit_gate}` and is required for commit and abort acknowledgements. `NeverRegisteredFloor` proves only staged generations were never registered. `ClosedAttemptEvidenceBundle` strongly owns every terminal outcome, decision/publication, admitted-shard apply/release ack, overlap-close, and capability/audit/backup/replay/remote-retention proof needed for compaction. `ClosedAttemptCompactionSpec` carries that bundle plus exact prior floor/state/conflict basis and a prebuilt `TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot` containing capability-safe token/attempt tombstones, terminal effect/reason commitments, and authenticated membership/nonmembership proofs. Apply verifies the heavy bundle, then creates `ClosedAttemptCompactionFloor {SameGroupCertificateHeader,through_global_prefix,terminal_summary_root_ref:StrongRef<TerminalAttemptSummaryRoot>,retained_active_attempt_commitment,still_live_obligation_refs[StrongRef],meta_checkpoint_identity:WeakDigest,quorum_signatures}`; it contains no strong/CRSR path back to compacted decision/prepare evidence. `GlobalClosedAttemptFloorInstallSpec` is `InstallNeverRegistered|InstallClosedCompaction{spec_ref:StrongRef<ClosedAttemptCompactionSpec>}`. Once its command is checkpoint-cut, heavy evidence can release subject to independent live floors, while late duplicate/status lookups resolve through the summary proofs. Neither floor decides or aborts prepared work.

`MetaConfigurationTransitionSpec` is `{phase:ProposeJoint|CommitJoint|CommitNew|CommitRetirementFloor,basis_global_state:WeakStateIdentity,current_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,prospective_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,candidate_closure_proof_ref:StrongRef,expected_global_prefix,expected_topology_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,resulting_topology_body_digest,paired_checkpoint_ref:StrongRef<GlobalRecoveryCheckpoint>?,paired_floor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConfigPayloadFloor>,required_certificate/remote/prepared_ownership_transfer floor,terminal_audit_gate}`. Deterministic apply constructs a `TopologyState` successor with identical epoch, form, shard assignments, and routing but the phase-appropriate current/joint/new `meta_configuration_ref` plus this applied control; no topology object may retain the retired meta configuration as current. Every phase is separate, and `CommitRetirementFloor` proves the new set owns all meta, prepared, certificate, and certified-remote obligations. `PreparedOwnershipTransferRecord` binds `{old/new prepared_ownership_ids,old/new configuration refs,identical base closure digest,old/new availability certificates,command/order status,transition floor}`; a current prepared root may carry a prior-config entry only in this explicit transfer state, and old ownership releases only after new ownership plus Raft/snapshot/apply/GC acknowledgement.

Shard membership is meta-authorized and later meta-adopted. `ShardReconfigurationAuthorizationSpec` is `{shard_id,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,old_configuration_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,joint/final canonical configuration bytes and digests,transition_nonce,payload_predicates,required_checkpoint/floor/remote/prepared/certificate obligations,terminal_audit_gate}`; its applied `ShardReconfigurationAuthorizationRecord` fixes the one permitted transition. Each `ShardConfigurationTransitionSpec` consumes the certified record and transfers every old-config owner. After `CommitRetirementFloor`, old+new quorums sign `ShardConfigurationAdoptionEvidence {SameGroupCertificateHeader,authorization_identity,old/joint/new configuration identities,final_floor,through_shard_index/global_prefix,remote_obligation_commitment,old_and_new_quorum_signatures}`. `ShardConfigurationAdoptionSpec` is meta input `{authorization_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,adoption_evidence_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardConfigurationAdoptionEvidence>,expected_topology_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,expected_old_shard_configuration_ref:RemoteConfigurationRef,new_configuration_evidence_ref:StrongRef<RemoteAuthorityConfigurationEvidence>,old_grant_release_plan,terminal_audit_gate}`. Apply creates the topology successor replacing exactly that shard entry; only then may the six-stage handshake release the old configuration grant and membership.

Distributed GC is a four-stage protocol, not paired one-shot proposals. A shard first orders `ShardGcPreflightSpec`; apply creates `ShardGcPreflightRecord {SameGroupCertificateHeader,basis_shard_state/root/index/global_prefix,topology_epoch,generated roots/cuts/prepared/certificate/lease/key/derived/backup/replay/remote inventories,exact_candidate_local_reclaim_set,excluded_obligations}` and its quorum exports `ShardGcPreflightEvidence`. Meta orders `GlobalGcAuthorizationSpec {basis_global_state/global_prefix,meta configuration/topology,typed_global_inventory,exact_global_local_reclaim_set,sorted_preflight_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardGcPreflightEvidence>],exact_per_shard_candidate_commitments,excluded_global obligations,remote_release_plan,terminal_audit_gate}`; its applied `GlobalGcAuthorizationRecord` authorizes only those sets and cannot itself release a remote target. Each shard then orders `ShardGcApplySpec {authorization_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalGcAuthorizationRecord>,preflight_ref:StrongRef<ShardGcPreflightRecord>,unchanged_or_stronger_basis,exact_local_reclaim_set,completed_remote_release_ack_refs[]}`; follower recomputation must be identical. Durable accepting apply creates the local decision, and physical reclaim may begin only afterward. The quorum exports `ShardGcAppliedAck {SameGroupCertificateHeader,authorization_identity,post_apply_state_root/index/global_prefix,reclaimed_inventory_digest,retained_exclusion_digest,completed_two_sided_release_commitment}`. Finally meta orders `GlobalGcCompletionSpec` with every required certified ack and records `Completed` or explicit `PartialBlocking`; it never claims a missing shard complete. Reconfiguration, checkpoints, and backup root every in-flight stage. Tests cover stale preflights, config/topology change, missing acks, crash immediately before/after local reclaim, and remote-release interleavings.

Effects use a two-stage acyclic construction. A shard first builds `ShardEffectBasis {global_txn_id,registration_generation,shard_id,registered_snapshot,topology_epoch,active_meta_projection_root_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,sorted_coordinate_bindings,write_key_material_projection_refs[StrongRef<ShardKeyMaterialProjection>],final_effect_refs[ConditionalCoordinateRef],logical_delta_fragment_template_ref:StrongRef<LogicalDeltaTemplate>,read_witness_refs[StrongRef],final_write_summary,constraint_requests_and_deltas,resource_charge_basis,authority_projection_digest,intent_semantics_oid,basis_effect_digest}`. Prepared traversal follows the conditional effect refs strongly; after the global marker assigns the commit coordinate, only matching activated/provisional effect cuts may stop them, while partition versions, delta leases, backup, and replay roots independently retain what remains promised. `basis_effect_digest` hashes the effect-only projection through `intent_semantics_oid`; it excludes every authorization decision, audit object, outcome preparation, resource transition object, fragment wrapper, prepare record, and certificate. `ParticipantRoutingDerivationProof` is `{topology_state_ref:StrongRef,initial_footprint_commitment,ordered_fixed_point_rounds[{round,prior_participant_set,discovered_cross_partition_effects,discovered_cascades,discovered_constraint_owners,resulting_participant_set}],final_read_write_cascade_constraint_footprint,partition_function_oid,proof_checker_version}`. Meta reaches that deterministic fixed point and builds `ParticipantRoutingCertificate {registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,topology_state_ref:StrongRef,sorted_basis_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>],sorted_participants,sorted_constraint_owners,complete_read_write_cascade_constraint_footprint,partition_derivation_proof_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingDerivationProof>,complete_participant_commitment,aggregate_template_digest,global_final_effect_digest}`, where `global_final_effect_digest = H("fgdb:global-effect:v1", sorted(shard_id,basis_effect_digest))`. Missing or extra bases/owners, a non-fixed-point cascade, or an unsupported routing proof fails closed.

Meta then builds exactly one standalone `GlobalAuthorizationDecisionRecord {registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,mutation_permit_ref:StrongRef<MutationPermitRecord>,authority_ceiling_digest,routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>,sorted_basis_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>],global_final_effect_digest,expected_branch_heads,expected_branch_key_epochs,constraint_and_resource_basis_commitment,policy_epoch,revocation_index,decision,authorization_audit_gate:AuthorizationAuditGate}`. It is a distinct W12 kind. The global validator replays the permit across the union, including hidden cascades and disclosure contracts; per-shard approvals cannot substitute. Meta next creates resource transitions, `GlobalTxnOutcomePreparationRecord`, one pending `AuditTicket`, and the immutable transaction audit-basis commitment—but no outcome event, resolution, or terminal gate yet. Admission orders and publishes that exact pending bundle. Only then may a participant build `ShardEffectFragment {basis_ref,prepare_admission_record_ref,admission_generation,routing_certificate_ref,global_authorization_ref,global_resource_transition_refs,global_outcome_preparation_ref,pending_audit_ticket_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<AuditTicket>,transaction_audit_basis_commitment,fragment_envelope_digest}`. The admission identifies all exact objects/commitments and includes this shard; the envelope digest is excluded from `global_final_effect_digest`. Prepare certificates bind the pending ticket/basis. After certification chooses Commit or Abort, Meta builds the matching `TransactionMutation` or typed no-effect/failure event, terminal resolution, and `TerminalAuditGate`, places that gate only in `GlobalTxnCommand`, and decision/shard apply verify it against the pending ticket/basis. No unused prebuilt terminal event exists to abandon.

`ShardPrepareCommand` is fence-free canonical input `{command_version,registration_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,prepare_admission_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,admission_generation,admission_global_logical_command_seq,admission_global_commit_seq,expected_prior_global_applied_prefix,routing_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>,basis_ref:StrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>,fragment_ref:StrongRef<ShardEffectFragment>,active_meta_projection_root_ref:StrongRef<ActiveMetaProjectionRoot>,shard_payload_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardPayloadAvailabilityCertificate>,expected_shard_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,expected_topology_epoch,expected_policy_epoch,expected_revocation_index,expected_branch_heads,expected_branch_key_epochs,prepare_key:{global_txn_id,registration_generation,admission_generation},local_prepare_generation}`. Before ordering, the shard first advances through every global command up to and including the unique admission—typed projection for every relevant control and exhaustive irrelevance proof otherwise—then verifies the active meta projection, topology/policy/revocation/key/audit state, configuration, admission, basis, and fragment byte-for-byte. Prepare does not advance that prefix a second time. A stale projection or matching abort tombstone rejects. Apply builds `ShardPrepareRecord {command_ref:StrongRef<ShardPrepareCommand|ShardDecisionApplyCommand>,prepare_key,shard_id,shard_configuration_ref:StrongRef<ConfigurationState>,topology_epoch,admission_global_prefix,local_prepare_generation,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<ShardPrepareRecord>?,basis_ref:StrongRef<ShardEffectBasis>,fragment_ref:StrongRef<ShardEffectFragment>,reservation_refs[StrongRef<ConstraintReservationRecord>],base/current_closure_inventory,state:Prepared|GloballyCommitted{global_logical_command_seq,global_commit_seq,decision_identity}|GloballyAborted{global_logical_command_seq,decision_identity}|Applied{global_logical_command_seq,global_commit_seq?,decision_identity,fragment_batch_ref:StrongRef<LogicalDeltaBatch>?}|GcEligible{terminal_floor_ref:StrongRef}}` and atomically installs the canonical constraint reservations plus a `ShardCommandRecord`; no local fence appears in either. Successors preserve the base inventory and strengthen the current closure. The shard-group `ShardPrepareCertificate` then quorum-signs its `SameGroupCertificateHeader` plus `{prepare_record_ref,admission/registration/routing remote identities,prepare_key,admission_generation/admission global prefix,shard/topology/active-projection identities,registered snapshot,expected heads/key epochs,basis/fragment/global-effect/witness/write/constraint/resource/authorization/audit commitments,payload_availability_certificate_ref,verifier_version,quorum_signatures}`. Followers recompute all fields. A late prepare after an abort tombstone, a second admission generation under one registration, or any mismatched/stale admission/routing/fragment/security projection is rejected; the later decision adds its assigned global sequence.

`ConstraintReservationRecord` is an owner-shard object `{reservation_id,constraint_id,canonical_domain_key_or_range,owner_shard,topology_epoch,prepare_key,registration_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,prepare_admission_record_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,routing_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>,exact_global_basis_digest,before_contribution,after_contribution,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<ConstraintReservationRecord>?,state:Held|Consumed{global_decision_identity}|Released{global_decision_identity}}`. `GlobalConstraintReservationCertificate` is produced by that owner shard after prepare and quorum-signs `{reservation_record_ref:StrongRef<ConstraintReservationRecord>,prepare_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ShardPrepareCertificate>,admission_record_remote_identity,constraint/domain/owner/topology identities,prepare_key,exact_global_basis_digest,before/after contribution,registered_snapshot,expiration:None,quorum_signatures}`. Meta receives it only as a certified-remote ref.

For a constraint whose topology declares meta ownership, admission apply creates `MetaConstraintReservationRecord {reservation_id,constraint_id,canonical_domain_key_or_range,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,admission_spec_ref:StrongRef<GlobalPrepareAdmissionSpec>,admission_generation,exact_global_basis_digest,before_aggregate,after_aggregate,predecessor_ref:StrongRef<MetaConstraintReservationRecord>?,state:Held|Consumed{global_txn_command_ref:StrongRef<GlobalTxnCommand>,global_logical_command_seq}|Released{applied_abort_ref:AppliedAbortRef}}` from the spec's pre-order request. `ConstraintReservationRef` is the closed tag `LocalMeta{reservation_ref:StrongRef<MetaConstraintReservationRecord>} | RemoteShard{reservation_certificate_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef<GlobalConstraintReservationCertificate>}`. `GlobalTxnCommand::Commit` names the exact complete sorted set; meta apply consumes local reservations atomically and each shard decision consumes its remote reservations. Abort names whatever remote certificates already exist, releases all meta reservations, and sends the published abort to every admitted shard so a present or late reservation cannot survive. Reservations are acquired in canonical order; clock timeout, suspicion, or coordinator loss has no effect.

`DistributedSerializationCertificate` is meta-owned and sequence-neutral `{attempt_key:{global_txn_id,registration_generation},lifecycle_basis:ReadOnly{read_routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ReadParticipantRoutingCertificate>}|ReadWrite{prepare_admission_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,admission_generation,routing_certificate_ref:StrongRef<ParticipantRoutingCertificate>},expected_global_logical_command_seq,conflict_index_basis:WeakStateIdentity,conflict_index_basis_digest:WeakDigest,overlapping_attempt_key_set_commitment,candidate_read_witness_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],candidate_write_summary_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],candidate_edges[{kind:wr|ww|rw,from_attempt_key,to_attempt_key,witness_or_version_proof_ref:CertifiedRemoteStrongRef}],retained_graph_projection_digest,scc_verifier_version,acyclic_result,conservative_fallbacks[],certifier_signature}`. `GlobalConflictIndex` is `{basis_global_logical_command_seq,entries[(global_txn_id,registration_generation) -> {snapshot/start/terminal prefixes,state:Active|PrepareAdmitted|Committed|Aborted|ReadClosed,admission_generation?,participants,read_witness_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],write_summary_refs[CertifiedRemoteStrongRef],incoming/outgoing_edges,overlap_close_floor}],safe_snapshot_frontier}`. Every meta follower reconstructs both directions of `may_affect`, verifies every routed shard/constraint contribution, and reruns the registered SCC algorithm; stale/missing support rejects. `GlobalAttemptIndex`, `GlobalTxnOutcomeIndex`, and the matching conflict entry must make the same lifecycle transition atomically. A new registration generation never overwrites an older overlapping generation; each entry remains rooted until its own overlap-close rule proves no future registered transaction can add an edge.

`GlobalTxnCommand` is the closed union with common `{command_version,registration_ref:StrongRef<GlobalAttemptRegistration>,prepare_admission_record_ref:StrongRef<GlobalControlRecord>,admission_generation,meta_pre_command_base_availability_certificate_ref:StrongRef<MetaPreCommandBaseAvailabilityCertificate>,expected_global_logical_command_seq,topology_state_ref:StrongRef<TopologyState>,policy_epoch,revocation_index,proposed_physical_hlcs[]}` and exactly one intent.
